langganan mugshot	subscribe to mugshot
Dupi jauh tina garéja ka stasion	Is it far from the church to the station
Peryogi sakitar 10 menit ku beus.	It takes about 10 minutes by bus.
Punten kirang langkung 10 menit.	It's a 10-minute walk.
Gareja aya dina jarak kajauhan.	The church is within walking distance.
Naon cara anu paling saé pikeun stasiun?	What's the best way to the station?
Dimana tempat ngantosan beus anu paling caket?	Where is the nearest bus stop?
Dimana lirén beus anu salajengna	Where is the next bus stop
Anjeun dina bus	You are on the bus
Anjeun moal tiasa sono éta.	You can't miss it.
Dadah.	See you.
Dupi sadayana kamar ngagaduhan AC?	Do all the rooms have air-conditioning?
Dupi sarapan atos kalebet?	Is breakfast included?
Iraha anjeun nyayogikeun sarapan?	When do you serve breakfast?
"Dupi anjeun tiasa nyauran kuring tabuh 7 énjing énjing, punten?	Could you give me a call at 7 tomorrow morning, please?"
Abdi hoyong mayar kontan / ku kartu kiridit / ku cék palancong	I'd like to pay in cash/by credit card/by traveller's cheque
"Halo, tiasa ngabantosan anjeun?	Hello, can I help you?"
Dupi anjeun hoyong kamar anu aya kamar ibak atanapi pancuran?	Would you like a room with a bath or a shower?
Sabaraha lami anjeun cicing di hotél kami?	How long would you like to stay at our hotel?
Kumaha anjeun badé mayar?	How would you like to pay?
Ruang anjeun aya di lantai kadua dina beulah katuhu.	Your room is on the second floor on the right.
"Hapunten, kami parantos dipesen wengi ayeuna	Sorry, we're fully booked for tonight."
"Hapunten, kami pinuh.	Sorry, we are full up. "
Aya naon waé anu kuring bisa laksanakeun pikeun anjeun?	Is there anything else I can do for you?
"Méja kanggo dua, punten.	A table for two, please."
Dupi kami tiasa calik di tabel ieu?	May we sit at this table?
"Menu ieu, punten.	The menu, please."
Naon di ménu?	What's on the menu?
Naon sapertos Irlandia Stew?	What's Irish Stew like?
Kami henteu acan siap.	We're not ready yet.
"Puncil kanggo abdi, punten.	The steak for me, please."
"Dupi anjeun tiasa pangnyandakeun abdi kénging, punten?	Can you bring me the ketchup, please?"
"Salad hiji, punten.	A salad, please."

Hasilna, éta ngarobih leuweung ku sungutna dibuka.	One day while Eklavya is practicing, he hears a dog barking. At first, the boy ignored the dog, but the continuous disturbance in his practice angered him. He stopped his practice and went towards the place where the dog was barking.  Before the dog could shut up or get out of the way, Eklavya fired seven arrows in rapid succession to fill the dog’s mouth without injuring it. As a result, it roamed the forests with its mouth opened."

 Éta saé!	 That’s great!

 Saé pisan!	 That’s wonderful!
 Luar biasa!	 Incredible!
 Éndah! Hatur nuhun pikeun ngabagi.	 Wonderful! Thank you for sharing.
 Emang? Anjeun serius?	 Really? Are you serious?
 Abdi henteu tiasa percanten yén!	 I can’t believe that!
Abdi sieun aya anu ngagaduhan béja anu goréng pikeun anjeun ...	I’m afraid I’ve got some bad news for you…
 Abdi hapunten tapi ...	 I’m so sorry but…
 Hapunten kuring parantos ngawartosan anjeun…	 I’m sorry to have to tell you that …
 Abdi terang ieu sanés upami anjeun hoyong ngadangu tapi…	 I know this isn’t what you want to hear but…
 Abdi sieun ngawartosan anjeun…	 I’m afraid to inform you of …
 Éta tugas kuring anu musibah pikeun nyarioskeun ka anjeun yén…	 It is my unfortunate duty to tell you that …
" Abdi leres-leres badé nyarios kieu, tapi…	 I really feel bad to have to say this, but …"
" Nyaan kuring henteu terang kumaha ngomongna, tapi…	 I really don’t know how to say it, but …"
Ngabales béja anu goréng:	Responding to bad news:
 Hapunten ngadangu yén ...	 I’m sorry to hear that…
 Anjeun kedah ngaraos pikasieuneun…	 You must be feeling terrible …
 Anu matak!	 That’s awful!
 Hanjakal!	 Too bad!
 Miskin anjeun!	 Poor you!
" Punten, nampi simpati kuring anu paling jero.	 Please, accept my deepest sympathy."
" Iraha waé anjeun kedah ngobrol, ukur nelepon kuring…	 Anytime you need to talk, just call me …"
" Upami aya naon anu abdi tiasa laksanakeun, hayu atuh terang…	 If there’s anything I can do, just let me know…"
 Éta goréng teuing.	 That’s too bad.
 Kumaha nguciwakeun!	 How disappointing!
 Éta nguciwakeun!	 That’s so disappointing!
" Oh moal, éra!	 Oh no, what a shame!"
 Éta éra hébat.	 It’s a great shame.
" Éta rada nguciwakeun, sanés!	 It’s a little bit disappointing, isn’t it!"
 Éta henteu hirup kana ekspektasi abdi.	 It didn’t live up to my expectations.
 Karunya pisan!	 What a pity!
 Naon letdown!	 What a letdown!
 Naon bummer!	 What a bummer!
 Éta gangguan	 That’s a nuisance!
 Abdi panginten anjeun tiasa ngalakukeun anu saé.	 I thought you could do better.
 Kuring teu pernah kuciwa dina kahirupan kuring.	 I’ve never been so disappointed in my life.
 Éta henteu saé siga anu panginten éta.	 It wasn’t as good as I thought it would be.
 Kumaha carana kuring…?	 How do I…?
 Naha anjeun tiasa nunjukkeun kumaha ...?	 Can you show me how to…?
 Naha anjeun terang kumaha…?	 Do you know how to…?
 Kumaha kuring ngauyang…?	 How do I go about…?
 Naon anu anjeun nyarankeun?	 What do you suggest?
 Naon léngkah munggaran?	 What is the first step?
 Naon cara anu pangsaéna pikeun…?	 What is the best way to…?
Masihan petunjuk:	Giving instructions:
" Anu mimiti, anjeun…	 First, you…"
" Teras anjeun…	 Then, you…"
" Teras, anjeun…	 Next, you…"
" Anu terakhir, anjeun…	 Lastly, you…"
Dimimitian kaluar:	Starting out:
 Hal kahiji anjeun lakukeun nyaéta…	 The first thing you do is…
" Sateuacan ngawitan, (anjeun kedah…)	 Before you begin, (you should…)"
 Tempat anu paling hadé pikeun dimimitian nyaéta…	 The best place to begin is…
 Abdi bakal ngamimitian ku…	 I would start by…
Nuluykeun:	Continuing:
" Saatos éta,	 After that,"
 Lengkah saterusna nyaéta…	 The next step is to…
 Hal anu anjeun lakukeun nyaéta…	 The next thing you do is…
" Sakali anjeun parantos ngalakukeun éta, maka…	 Once you’ve done that, then…"
" Nalika anjeun réngsé éta, maka…	 When you finish that, then…"
Pagawean:	Finishing:
 Léngkah terakhir nyaéta…	 The last step is…
 Hal anu anjeun lakukeun nyaéta…	 The last thing you do is…
" Tungtungna,…	 In the end,…"
" Nalika tos réngsé,…	 When you’ve finished,…"
" Nalika tos réngsé sagala léngkah,…	 When you’ve completed all the steps,…"
 Éta kalepatan	 It’s your fault.
 Éta kalepatan anjeun.	 It’s your mistake.
 Abdi henteu tiasa percanten yén anjeun ngalakukeun éta.	 I can’t believe that you did it.
 Kumaha anjeun tiasa ngalakukeun hal sapertos kitu?	 How could you do such a thing?
 Naha anjeun kaluar tina pikiran anjeun?	 Are you out of your mind?
 Naon di bumi anu anjeun pikir?	 What on earth were you thinking?
 Kuring anggap anjeun salah anu nyalahkeun.	 I think you are the one to blame.
 Kuring anggap anjeun mangrupikeun saha anu tiasa dilakukeun.	 I think you are the one who could have done it.
Babasan of Tuduh Jalma:	Expressions of Accusing Someone:
 Éta pasti anjeun anu ngalakukeun éta.	 It must have been you who did it.
 Kuring pikir anjeun mangrupikeun hiji-hijina jalma anu tiasa ngalakukeun éta.	 I think you’re the only person who could have done it.
 Anjeun kedah ngalakukeun anu salah.	 You must be doing something wrong.
Narima nyalahkeun sareng nuduh:	Accepting blaming and accusing:
 Abdi nyungkeun hapunten. Éta kalepatan abdi.	 I’m sorry. It’s my fault.
 Hapunten kanggo hal anu parantos dilakukeun.	 I’m sorry for the things I’ve done.
 Abdi hapunten Abdi henteu hartosna.	 I’m really sorry. I didn’t mean to.
 Hapunten lepat abdi.	 Sorry for my fault.
 Éta tanggung jawab kuring. Abdi nyungkeun hapunten.	 It’s my responsibility. I’m sorry.
 Anjeun leres! Éta kalepatan abdi. Abdi nyungkeun hapunten.	 You’re right! It’s my fault. I’m sorry.
Nolak nyalahkeun sareng nuduh:	Refusing blaming and accusing:
 Éta henteu leres.	 It’s not true.
 Éta henteu salah kuring.	 It’s not my fault.
 Abdi sanés urang anu nyalahkeun	 I’m not the one to blame.
 Abdi henteu ngalakukeun éta.	 I didn’t do it.
 Anjeun salah. Éta sanés.	 You’re wrong. It wasn’t me.

Hiji dinten hujan tiis	One cold rainy day
nalika bapak kuring masih budak leutik	when my father was a little boy
anjeunna tepang sareng ucing gang lami di jalanna	he met an old alley cat on his street
Ucing-ucing téh kacida luh	The cat was very drippy
sareng teu pikaresepeun	and uncomfortable 
kitu saur bapa kuring	so my father said
Dupi anjeun hoyong angkat sareng abdi	Would you like to come home with me
Ieu kaget ucing	This surprised the cat
anjeunna henteu kantos kantos tepang saha waé	she had never before met anyone 
anu paduli ucing gang lami	who cared about old alley cats
ceuk manehna	she said
Atuh janten pisan wajib	I would be very much obliged 
upami kuring tiasa calik ku hawu haneut	if I could sit by a warm furnace
panginten gaduh saos susu	perhaps have a saucer of milk
Kami ngagaduhan tungku anu saé kanggo didaptarkeun	We have a very nice furnace to sit by
Kuring yakin indung kuring ngagaduhan piring susu tambahan.	I am sure my mother has an extra saucer of milk.
Bapa sareng ucing kuring	My father and the cat
janten rerencangan anu saé	became good friends 
tapi bapak kuring rada kesel	but my father was very upset 
ngeunaan ucing	about the cat
Anjeunna na hate ucing	She hated cats
utamina pisan	particularly ugly
kucing ucing lami	old alley cats
saurna ka bapa	she said to my father
lamun anjeun pikir	if you think
pasihan ucing éta	give that cat 
aya saos susu	a saucer of milk
anjeun salah pisan	you are very wrong
Sakali anjeun mimiti tuang	Once you start feeding
nyasar gang ucing	stray alley cats 
anjeun ogé nyangka ogé	you might as well expect 
pikeun nyayogikeun unggal nyasar di kota	to feed every stray in town
Kuring moal bade ngalakukeun éta	I am not going to do it
Ieu dilakukeun bapak kuring	This made my father 
hanjelu pisan	very sad
anjeunna ngahaturkeun ka ucing	he apologized to the cat 
indungna kungsi jadi kurang ajar	his mother had been so rude
Anjeunna ngawartoskeun ucing	He told the cat
tinggal baé	stay anyway
éta kumaha waé anjeunna bakal mawa anjeunna	that somehow he would bring her
saos susu unggal dinten	a saucer of milk each day
Bapa kuring nyusian ucing	My father fed the cat
salila tilu minggu	for three weeks
"hiji poé, indungna mendakan saucer di gudang di jero taneuh	one day his mother found the saucer in the cellar"
anjeunna pisan ambek	she was extremely angry
Anjeunna ngusapan bapa kuring	She whipped my father 
ngalungkeun ucing kaluar panto	threw the cat out the door
engke bapa kuring nyarios kaluar	later on my father sneaked out 
mendakan ucing	found the cat
Duaan aranjeunna leumpang	Together they went for a walk
di taman	in the park
manéh mikir kana hal-hal anu saé	tried to think of nice things
pikeun ngobrol ngeunaan	to talk about
Nalika kuring dewasa	When I grow up 
Abdi angkat pesawat	I am going to have an airplane
Naha tiasa saé anu ngapung	Would it be wonderful to fly
ngan dimana waé anjeun panginten	just anywhere you might think of
Dupi anjeun hoyong ngapung pisan	Would you like to fly very much
Kuring pasti	I certainly would
Kuring bakal ngalakukeun nanaon	I would do anything 
upami abdi tiasa ngapung	if I could fly
Nya	Well
Upami anjeun hoyong pisan	If you would really like
ngapung anu jauh	to fly that much
Sigana kuring terang	I think I know
hiji tempat anu jauh	a sort of away
anjeun tiasa nyandak	you might get
mabur bari anjeun masih alit kénéh	to fly while you are still a little boy
Maksudna anjeun terang	You mean you know
dimana kuring tiasa	where I could 
kéngingkeun kapal terbang	get an airplane
teu persis kapal terbang	not exactly an airplane
tapi aya hal anu langkung saé	but something even better
Sakumaha anjeun tiasa tingali	As you can see
Abdi ucing lami	I am an old cat
di dinten ngora kuring	in my younger days
Abdi rada saémbara	I was quite a traveler
Dinten abdi angkat na langkung	My traveling days are over
cinyusu panungtungan kuring nyandak hiji deui perjalanan	last spring I took just one more trip
balayar ka hiji Pulo	sailed to a Island 
lirén dina palabuhan	stopping at the port
euy jadi kajadian	it just so happened 
Abdi teu sono kana kapal	I missed the boat
sareng bari ngantosan salajengna	and while waiting for the next 
Teu sangka kuring bakal katingali sakedik	I thought I would look around a bit
Abdi khususna kabetot	I was particularly interested
Dina hiji tempat	In a place 
anu ku urang parantos maot	which we had passed 
dina perjalanan kami	on our way 
ngahiji	joined together 
ku senar panjang batu	by a long string of rocks
jalma henteu kantos ka Pulau Wild	people never go to Wild Island 
éta biasana leuweung	it is mostly jungle 
dicicingan ku sato galak pisan	inhabited by very wild animals
Janten kuring mutuskeun merentasi batu	So I decided to go across the rocks
ngajajah éta pikeun kuring	explore it for me
Éta pasti mangrupikeun tempat anu pikaresepeun	It certainly is an interesting place
Kuring ningali aya anu aya	I saw something there 
anu dilakukeun kuring hoyong ceurik	that made me want to weep

Anjeunna ngangkat daging sareng katangkep dina perangkap.	He picked the meat and got caught in the trap.
Di jalak	The jackal
disebut sasatoan sato	called all the animals
sareng ningal aranjeunna rubah sareng saur	and showed them the fox and said
Upami a	If a 
raja	king
moal tiasa ngontrol kahayang na	cannot control his desires
sareng percaya batur tanpa mikir	and believes others without thinking
anjeunna henteu kantos tiasa janten pimpinan anu saé.	he can never be a good leader
Dina hiji waktu	ONCE upon a time
aya pangeran anu hoyong nikah ku putri	there was a prince who wanted to marry a princess
tapi anjeunna kedah janten putri nyata	but she would have to be a real princess
Anjeunna ngumbara ka sadaya penjuru dunya	He traveled all over the world to find one
tapi dimana waé anjeunna tiasa nampi naon anu dipikahoyong	but nowhere could he get what he wanted
Aya putri cukup	There were princesses enough
tapi hese pikeun terang naha aranjeunna nyata	but it was difficult to find out whether they were real ones
sok aya hal ngeunaan aranjeunna anu henteu sapertos anu sakuduna	there was always something about them that was not as it should be
Janten anjeunna mulih deui sareng hanjelu	So he came home again and was sad
pikeun anjeunna bakal resep pisan pikeun gaduh putri nyata	for he would have liked very much to have a real princess
Hiji wengi badai anu dahsyat sumping	One evening a terrible storm came on
aya guruh sareng kilat	there were thunder and lightning
jeung hujan turun dina banjir	and the rain poured down in torrents
Ujug-ujug nguping kadenge di gapura kota	Suddenly a knocking was heard at the city gate
sareng raja lami angkat ngabuktoskeun	and the old king went to open it
Éta putri ngadeg di luar gapuraeun	It was a princess standing out there in front of the gate
Tapi	But
saenggeusna	good gracious
naon tetempoan hujan sareng angin ngajantenkeun dirina	what a sight the rain and the wind had made her look
cai lumpat turun tina rambut sareng baju	the water ran down from her hair and clothes
éta lumpat kana toes sapatu na kaluar deui di tumit	it ran down into the toes of her shoes and out again at the heels
Tatang saur anjeunna yén anjeunna putri nyata	And yet she said that she was a real princess
Nya	Well
urang bakal enggal mendakan éta	we will soon find that out
panginten ratu lawas	thought the old queen
"Tapi uing ngomong euweuh, indit ka pangkengna	But she said nothing, went into the bedroom"
nyandak sadaya tempat tidur dina ranjang	took all the bedding off the bedstead
sareng neundeun kacang polong dina handapeun	and laid a pea on the bottom
teras manehna nyandak dua puluh kasur sareng neundeun kana kacang polong na	then she took twenty mattresses and laid them on the pea
sareng dua puluh ranjang anu langkung handap dina kasur	and then twenty eider-down beds on top of the mattresses
Dina ieu	On this
putri kedah ngabohong sapeuting wengi	the princess had to lie all night
Isuk-isuk manéhna nanya kumaha manéhna saré	In the morning she was asked how she had slept
Oh	Oh
parah pisan	very badly
ceuk manéhna	said she
Kuring nembak ampir nutup panon kuring sapeuting	I have scarcely closed my eyes all night
Sawarga ngan ukur terang naon anu aya dina ranjang	Heaven only knows what was in the bed
tapi kuring bohong keras	but I was lying on something hard
janten abdi hideung sareng biru sadayana awak kuring	so that I am black and blue all over my body
Éta pikareueuseun	It is horrible
Ayeuna aranjeunna terang yén anjeunna putri nyata kusabab anjeunna parantos ngaraos kacang polong ngalangkungan dua puluh kasur sareng dua puluh ranjang anu handap	Now they knew that she was a real princess because she had felt the pea right through the twenty mattresses and the twenty eider-down beds
Teu aya anu namina tapi putri nyata tiasa sénsitip kana éta	Nobody but a real princess could be as sensitive as that
Janten pangeran nyandak dirina pikeun pamajikanana	So the prince took her for his wife
kanggo ayeuna	for now
anjeunna terang yén anjeunna gaduh putri nyata	he knew that he had a real princess
jeung kacang polong ieu dipasang dina musium	and the pea was put in the museum
"dimana éta masih katingal	where it may still be seen,"
lamun teu aya anu maok	if no one has stolen it
"Aya, éta mangrupikeun carita anu leres	There, that is a true story"
A Hare keur nyenangkeun tukang Toret hiji dinten sadinten alon	A Hare was making fun of the Tortoise one day for being so slow
Naha anjeun kantos angkat ka mana waé	Do you ever get anywhere
manehna nanya kalayan seuri ngoyak	he asked with a mocking laugh
Leres	Yes
jawab Si Kura-kura	replied the Tortoise
sareng abdi badé sumping langkung gancang ti anu anjeun pikir	and I get there sooner than you think
Kuring bakal ngajalankeun anjeun balapan sareng ngabuktikeun éta	I will run you a race and prove it
The Hare jauh pikaresepeun dina pamanggih ngajalankeun balapan sareng Tortoise	The Hare was much amused at the idea of running a race with the Tortoise
tapi pikeun kasenangan eta hal	but for the fun of the thing
anjeunna sapuk	he agreed
Janten Fox	So the Fox
anu parantos satuju pikeun ngajantenkeun hakim	who had consented to act as judge
ditandaan jarak jauh sareng ngamimitian para pelari pareum	marked the distance and started the runners off
Si Hare pas énggal teu katingali	The Hare was soon far out of sight
sareng ngadamel Tortoise rumasa jero pisan matak konyol kanggo anjeunna nyobian balapan sareng Hare	and to make the Tortoise feel very deeply how ridiculous it was for him to try a race with a Hare
anjeunna ngagolér di gigir waé pikeun nyandak sare dugi ka Tortoise kedah naék	he lay down beside the course to take a nap until the Tortoise should catch up
Samentara Tortoise tetep lalaunan tapi terus-terusan	The Tortoise meanwhile kept going slowly but steadily
jeung	and
saatos waktos	after a time
kaliwat tempat anu Hare saré	passed the place where the Hare was sleeping
Tapi Hare bobo bobo pisan	But the Hare slept on very peacefully
sareng nalika tungtungna anjeunna hudang	and when at last he did wake up
tempat Tortoise caket cita	the Tortoise was near the goal
Si Hare ayeuna lumpat ngagancangna	The Hare now ran his swiftest
tapi anjeunna henteu tiasa nyabutan tukangeun waktos na	but he could not overtake the Tortoise in time
Lalaunan sareng anteng menang balapan	Slow and steady wins the race
Dina hiji waktu	Once upon a time
wabah parna aya di tengah sato	a severe plague raged among the animals
Loba anu maot	Many died
jeung jalma anu hirup éta gering pisan	and those who lived were so ill
anu aranjeunna henteu ngayakeun tuangeun atanapi tuangeun	that they cared for neither food nor drink
sareng seret nyalira nyalira	and dragged themselves about listlessly
Teu lami tiasa ngagentos hayam bikang anu gemuk ngagoda Master Fox pikeun tuangeun	No longer could a fat young hen tempt Master Fox to dinner
atawa domba lembut henteu nyababkeun napsu Sir Wolf.	nor a tender lamb rouses greedy Sir Wolf's appetite.
Ahirna	At last
Singa mutuskeun pikeun nelepon dewan	the Lion decided to call a council
Nalika sadaya sasatoan ngariung éta ngahiji sareng anjeunna nyarios	When all the animals were gathered together he arose and said
Babaturan réréncangan	Dear friends
Kuring yakin déwa-déwa ngutus bala ieu janten hukuman pikeun dosa-dosa urang	I believe the gods have sent this plague upon us as a punishment for our sins
Ku alatan éta	Therefore
anu paling kaliru salah sahiji urang kedah disuguhan janten korban	the most guilty one of us must be offered in sacrifice
Panginten urang janten kéngingkeun pangampura sareng tamba pikeun sadayana	Perhaps we may thus obtain forgiveness and cure for all
Abdi bakal ngaku sadaya dosa kuring tiheula	I will confess all my sins first
Kuring ngaku yén kuring parah pisan rewog sareng ngahakan seueur domba	I admit that I have been very greedy and have devoured many sheep
Aranjeunna henteu dilakukeun kuring ngarugikeun	They had done me no harm
Kuring parantos mendakan embé sareng banténg sareng stags	I have eaten goats and bulls and stags
Ngabari kaleresan	To tell the truth
Kuring malah tuang pangangon ayeuna teras	I even ate up a shepherd now and then
Ayeuna	Now
lamun kuring paling kaliru	if I am the most guilty
Abdi parantos dikurbankeun	I am ready to be sacrificed
Tapi kuring nganggap yén paling hadé masing-masing ngaku dosa-Na sakumaha anu kuring parantos dilakukeun	But I think it best that each one confesses his sins as I have done
teras urang tiasa mutuskeun dina sagala kaadilan anu paling kaliru	then we can decide in all justice who is the most guilty
Kaluhuran anjeun	Your majesty
saur Fox	said the Fox
anjeun saé teuing	you are too good
Bisa waé jadi kajahatan dahar domba	Can it be a crime to eat sheep
sirah mutton sapertos bodo	such stupid mutton heads
Henteu	No
henteu	no
kaagungan anjeun	your majesty
Anjeun parantos ngajantenkeun aranjeunna ngahargaan pisan ku tuang aranjeunna	You have done them great honor by eating them up
Jeung sajauh anu angon prihatin	And so far as shepherds are concerned
urang sadayana terang éta milik ras puny yén anu jadi purwa kami	we all know they belong to that puny race that pretends to be our masters
Sakabeh sasatoan ditepokkeun Fox	All the animals applauded the Fox loudly
Satuluyna	Then
sanajan Macan	though the Tiger
si Bear	the Bear
kana Wolf	the Wolf
sareng sadaya sato galak bijil kana perbuatan anu paling jahat	and all the savage beasts recited the most wicked deeds
sadayana dibébaskeun sareng didamel siga pisan satia sareng murni	all were excused and made to appear very saint-like and innocent
Ayeuna éta giliran si Ass pikeun ngaku	It was now the Ass's turn to confess
Abdi émut	I remember
ceuk kasalahan	he said guiltily
éta hiji dinten nalika kuring ngalangkungan sawah milik sababaraha pandita	that one day as I was passing a field belonging to some priests
Kituna kuring digoda ku jukut lembut sareng lapar kuring	I was so tempted by the tender grass and my hunger
anu kuring teu tiasa nahan nyerbling sakedik éta	that I could not resist nibbling a bit of it
Abdi henteu kagungan hak ngalakukeun éta	I had no right to do it
Kuring ngaku	I admit
Gempa hébat diantara sato-sato ngaganggu anjeunna	A great uproar among the beasts interrupted him
Ieu mangrupikeun penjahat anu parantos kéngingkeun kasiksa	Here was the culprit who had brought misfortune on all of them
Kejahatan anu matak pikahitaeun nyaéta dahar jukut anu dipiboga jalma anu sanés	What a horrible crime it was to eat grass that belonged to someone else
Éta cukup ngagantung pikeun saha waé	It was enough to hang anyone for
langkung seueur hiji Ass	much more an Ass
Geuwat aranjeunna sadayana murag ka anjeunna	Immediately they all fell upon him
si Wolf dina nuju	the Wolf in the lead
sareng enggal-enggal parantos ngeureunkeun anjeunna	and soon had made an end to him
Kurban anjeunna ka déwa-déwa tuluy aya	sacrificing him to the gods then and there
sareng tanpa formalitas altar	and without the formality of an altar
Lemah dilakukeun pikeun sangsara ku kasalahan anu kawasa	The weak are made to suffer for the misdeeds of the powerful
Seueur taun ka pengker	Many years ago
aya Kaisar	there was an Emperor
anu kacida kaleuleuwihi ku baju anyar	who was so excessively fond of new clothes
yen anjeunna nganggo artos sadayana dina pakéan	that he spent all his money in dress
Anjeunna henteu ngaganggu dirina di paling saeutik ngeunaan tentara na	He did not trouble himself in the least about his soldiers
anjeunna teu paduli teras angkat ka téater atanapi ngudag	nor did he care to go either to the theatre or the chase
kecuali kasempetan anu teraskeun anjeunna pikeun nunjukkeun baju énggalna	except for the opportunities then afforded him for displaying his new clothes
Anjeunna ngagaduhan setelan anu béda pikeun unggal jam dina sapoe	He had a different suit for each hour of the day
sareng sakumaha raja atanapi Kaisar séjén	and as of any other king or emperor
salah saurang ogé biasa	one is accustomed to say

Kaisar calik dina papakéanna	The Emperor is sitting in his wardrobe
Waktosna kasorang merpily di kota gedé anu mangrupikeun ibukota	Time passed merrily in the large town which was his capital
urang asing sumping unggal dinten di pangadilan	strangers arrived every day at the court
Hiji dinten	One day
dua rogues	two rogues
nyebatna rangrang	calling themselves weavers

Aranjeunna masihan kaluar yén maranéhna terang kumaha ninun barang tina warna anu paling éndah sareng pola rumit	They gave out that they knew how to weave stuffs of the most beautiful colors and elaborate patterns
baju anu didamel tina mana anu ngagaduhan harta anu saé tetep anu teu katingali ku saha waé anu teu pantes kanggo kantor anu dicekel	the clothes manufactured from which should have the wonderful property of remaining invisible to everyone who was unfit for the office he held
atanapi anu biasa sacara sederhana dina karakter	or who was extraordinarily simple in character
Ieu kedah	These must
leres pisan	indeed
janten baju anu endah	be splendid clothes

Upami kedah jas kitu	Had I such a suit
Atuh sakaligus kuring mendakan naon lalaki di alam kuring anu pantes pikeun kantorna	I might at once find out what men in my realms are unfit for their office
sarta ogé tiasa ngabédakeun wicaksana tina akal budi	and also be able to distinguish the wise from the foolish
Barang ieu kedah dianggo langsung pikeun kuring	This stuff must be woven for me immediately
Sareng anjeunna nyababkeun jumlah artos anu ageung dipasihan pikeun para tukang tenun supados aranjeunna tiasa ngawitan damel langsung	And he caused large sums of money to be given to both the weavers in order that they might begin their work directly
Janten dua panenam anu nyamar dua nyetél dua geladak	So the two pretended weavers set up two looms
sareng kapangaruhan pikeun damel pisan bosen	and affected to work very busily
sanajan kanyataanana	though in reality

Aranjeunna ménta sutra anu paling alus sareng benang emas murni	They asked for the most delicate silk and the purest gold thread

sareng teras neruskeun pagawéan anu pura-pura dina looms kosong dugi ka wengi ayeuna	and then continued their pretended work at the empty looms until late at night
Abdi resep terang kumaha penenjang damel sareng lawon kuring	I should like to know how the weavers are getting on with my cloth

saatos sababaraha waktos sakedik parantos lami	after some little time had elapsed

kumaha oge	however

Pikeun mastikeun	To be sure

Sadaya jalma di sapanjang kota kagungan uninga tina harta anu saé anu dipakilén éta kaén	All the people throughout the city had heard of the wonderful property the cloth was to possess

Naon tiasa hartos ieu	What can be the meaning of this
